***aarzelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aarzelen.html>aarzelen</a> (12871)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">erselen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">arselen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to step back, to retreat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, frequentative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ersen</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aers</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">buttocks</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aars.html>aars</a></i>). Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">arsle</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aarzelen.html>aarzelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hesitate</li></ol>

***aas.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aas.html>aas</a> (5116)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">âes</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ās</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ēsaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>bait</li>
<li>carrion</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ase</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aes</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">as</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">as</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aas.html>aas</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:azen.html>azen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aas.html>aasje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">ace</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">playing cards</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">ace</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">skilled person</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> unit of mass corresponding to approximately 0.05 grams</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">ace</span>, any very small amount</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aas.html>aas</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">carrion</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gier.html>gier</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">vulture</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>Egyptian vulture, <i>Neophron percnopterus</i>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any vulture, especially one whose diet consists of carrion.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A vulture, a person who profits from the suffering of others.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:abnormaal.html>abnormaal</a> (11277)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">abnormal</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">abnormal</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ab-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:normaal.html>normaal</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:abnormaal.html>abnormaal</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:abnormaal.html>abnormaler</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">abnormaalst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>abnormal (not conforming to rule or system)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:abortus.html>abortus</a> (6215)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin">New Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:abortus.html>abortus</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">miscarriage</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:abortus.html>abortus</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:abortussen.html>abortussen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:abortus.html>abortusje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***abra.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:abra.html>abra</a> (41155)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Attested since 1440. Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">havre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">havene</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*habnō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">harvour, <a href = vnd.unilang:haven.html>haven</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="gl"><a href = vnd.unilang:abra.html>abra</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-gl p-form-of" lang="gl">abras</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>creek, inlet, bay
<ul><li><b>1440</b>, Miguel González Garcés (ed.), <i>Historia <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> La Coruña. Edad Media</i>. A Coruña: Caixa Galicia, page 619:
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> todo <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:porto.html>porto</a> et <b><a href = vnd.unilang:abra.html>abra</a></b> desta dita uilla</i>
<dl><dd>in the whole harbor and <b>bay</b> of <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> town</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***abracadabra.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:abracadabra.html>abracadabra</a> (19930)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:abracadabra.html>abracadabra</a></i>, a word used in magical writings, of uncertain origin. Relationships have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> suggested with <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:abraxas.html>Abraxas</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">a Gnostic deity</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and with various Aramaic or Hebrew <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">עברא כדברא</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">avra kedavra</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">what <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> come to pass</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Hebr mention" lang="arc">עַבְדָא כְּדַברָא</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="arc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">avda kedavara</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">what <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> done</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">ארבע-אחד-ארבע</i> |  (<i>arba-eḥad-arba</i>, literally “four-one-four”),<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> but there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> little supporting evidence.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:abracadabra.html>abracadabra</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">abracadabras</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A use of the mystical term ‘<a href = vnd.unilang:abracadabra.html>abracadabra</a>’, supposed to work as part of a healing charm or a magical spell; any spell or incantation making use of the word. <span class="defdate">[from 16th c.]</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1851</b>,  Hugh A. Garland, quoting <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Randolph_of_Roanoke" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Randolph of Roanoke">John Randolph of <a href = vnd.unilang:roanoke.html>Roanoke</a></a>,  “The Virginia Convention—Every Change <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> Not Reform”, in  <cite>The Life of John Randolph of <a href = vnd.unilang:roanoke.html>Roanoke</a></cite>, volume II, New York |  D. Appleton amp; Company, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/1965434">1965434</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=-8QEAAAAYAAJamp;pg=PA329">page 329</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Where <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the necessity of this provision in the Constitution? <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> Can anyone believe that <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a>, by any amendments of ours, by any of our scribbling on that parchment, by any <a href = vnd.unilang:amulet.html>amulet</a>, any legerdemain—charm—<b>Abrecadabra</b>—of ours can prevent our sons from doing the same thing—that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, from doing as they please, just as <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> are doing as <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> please? It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> impossible. Who can bind posterity?</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2012</b> August 28,  <a href = vnd.unilang:georgina.html>Georgina</a> Turner,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Guardian" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Guardian">The Guardian</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">With a quiet bank holiday afternoon to fill, the Mill yesterday dug out the old magic kit, brushed the cobwebs off its top hat and practiced a few <b>abracadabras</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>Mumbo-jumbo; obscure language or technicalities; jargon. <span class="defdate">[from 19th c.]</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">I don’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> know all the theoretical <b><a href = vnd.unilang:abracadabra.html>abracadabra</a></b> about how it works, I’m only its pilot.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1971</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Keith_Thomas_(historian)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Keith Thomas (historian)">Keith Thomas</a>,  <cite>Religion and the Decline of Magic</cite>, Folio Society 2012, page 335:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Astrology <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> not specifically banned in the statutes against witchcraft, but so long as its technicalities remained <b><a href = vnd.unilang:abracadabra.html>abracadabra</a></b> to the lay public there <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> always a risk that the practitioner might find himself arrested for sorcery.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:abracadabra.html>abracadabra</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Used to indicate that a magic trick or other illusion <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> performed.</span> <span class="defdate">[from 19th c.]</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hey.html>hey</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:presto.html>presto</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:abracadabra.html>abracadabra</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:wartaal.html>wartaal</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:onduidelijk.html>onduidelijke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:taal.html>taal</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sprak.html>sprak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hele.html>hele</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:abracadabra.html>abracadabra</a></b>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synoniemen"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:synoniemen.html>Synoniemen</a></i></span></h5>

</body>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">abricot</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">اَلْبَرْقُوق‎</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">al-barqūq</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">πραικόκιον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">praikókion</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">praecoqua</i>.

***abseil.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:abseil.html>abseil</a> (120112)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:abseilen.html>abseilen</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">ab-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">down</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Seil</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rope</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/abseil" class="extiw" title="w:abseil"><a href = vnd.unilang:abseil.html>abseil</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/abseil" class="extiw" title="w:abseil">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:abseil.html>abseil</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">abseils</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">abseiling</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">abseiled</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To descend a steep or vertical drop using a rope with a mechanical friction device or <i>(classic <a href = vnd.unilang:abseil.html>abseil</a>)</i> by wrapping the rope around the body; to <a href = vnd.unilang:rappel.html>rappel</a>. <span class="defdate">[First attested in the mid 20th century.]</span><sup id="cite_ref-SOED_1-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-SOED-1"> | 1 | </a></sup></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><a href = vnd.unilang:rappel.html>rappel</a></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">abseiler</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:abseil.html>abseil</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">abseils</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A descent in mountaineering using a rope looped at the top and a friction device. <span class="defdate">[First attested in the mid 20th century.]</span><sup id="cite_ref-SOED_1-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-SOED-1"> | 1 | </a></sup></li></ol>

<ul><li><a href = vnd.unilang:rappel.html>rappel</a></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:abseil.html>abseil</a></b>
</p>

***absint.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:absint.html>absint</a> (35378)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">absinthium</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">absinthium</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀψίνθιον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">apsínthion</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>In the current spelling from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">absinthe</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:absint.html>absint</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>absinthe (liquor)</li></ol>
<hr />
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***abuis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:abuis.html>abuis</a> (33585)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">abuus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">abus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">abūsus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:abuis.html>abuis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:abuis.html>abuizen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:abuis.html>abuisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>An error, a mistake.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A wrong, abuse, a wrongful action or activity.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A strange or miraculous phenomenon.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">per <a href = vnd.unilang:abuis.html>abuis</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:abuis.html>abuis</a></strong> (<i>used only predicatively</i>, <i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>mistaken, wrong</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:abuis.html>abuis</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>

***academie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:academie.html>academie</a> (5506)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">académie</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">acadēmīa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Ἀκαδημία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Akadēmía</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a grove of trees and gymnasium outside of Athens where <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Plato" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Plato">Plato</a> taught; from the name of the supposed former owner of that estate, the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Attica" class="extiw" title="w:Attica">Attic</a> hero <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Akademos" class="extiw" title="w:Akademos">Akademos</a>. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">achterbaecs</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">behind one's back</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<dl><dd>He really <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <b>sneaky</b> bastard.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>Acting "<a href = vnd.unilang:achterbaks.html>achterbaks</a>" <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> to act in a way you wouldn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> expect from well-behaved people, implied <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> little profit or benefit for the one doing it and big loss for the one it's done to.
</p>

<dl><dd>The collective helps the inhabitants of an impoverished area of Liverpool renovate premises that would be demolished otherwise by themselves.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
